3) what is BEP ..what are the assumptions of BEP

Unit 4

1) what is double entry book keeping system objectives advantages and disadvantages
2) what is accounting cycle 
3) discuss types of accounts and rules governing
4) explain accounting concepts and conventions 
5) problems from final account and general entries 
6) problem from ratio analysis



Unit 5
1) what are the various sources of financing 
2) what are the factors determining requirements of working capital
3) problem from working capital 
4) What is capital budgeting
5) advantages and disadvantages of capital budgeting

12/09/2022, 22:24 - Vishnu Sathwik: Dear  Students,
Find attached. It is mandatory for all III and V semester  students to register and onboard to  AICTE LITE Program in "Advanced Web Development"  which is free of cost and complete the WD101 and WD 201 courses within the deadline. Course completion certificate is accepted as Internship/ Activity points as per rules. 
Benefits and Procedure of the Course
Students who qualify the eligibility criteria and submit completed interest form will be onboarded to take the WD 101 by Pupilfirst free of cost.
Post completion of the WD 101 course, Pupifirst will onboard eligible students to the WD 201 course on a full scholarship basis.
Students who complete the WD 101 and WD 201 courses successfully, will be onboarded as TAs. During their work as a TA, they will be given a stipend and certificate for their contributions.
Working experience under Coaches of Pupilfirst and Industry experts
For admission details visit : https://wd.pupilfirst.org/
registration link : https://www.pupilfirst.school/courses/1802/apply

For any queries contact
